  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_41cd8a79-4012-465f-8af4-a8dd855f6585'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">The book is about young people that are sheltered and mistreated in their childhood with the dreams of "being somebody" when they made it to adulthood<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">The book is about young people that are sheltered and mistreated in their childhood with the dreams of "being somebody" when they made it to adulthood. Both have adventurous times in their reckless lives once they reach stardom. <br />It was been a while since I've read this book, but it's a good one! Note: I haven't been on GR in some time, so I am making up for lost time. :) <a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5185388948815012136">A Stranger in the Mirror, Sidney Sheldon<br/><br/>A Stranger in the Mirror is a 1976 novel written by American writer Sidney Sheldon. The novel is one of the earliest Sheldon's works, but contains the typical Sheldon fast-paced narration and several narrative techniques with the exception of a twist ending. <br/><br/>The novel tells the life story of two fictitious Hollywood celebrities - Toby Temple and Jill Castle portray the emotional extremes of success and failure and how people inevitably become victims of ti</span>
  <span id="freeText5185388948815012136" style="display:none">A Stranger in the Mirror, Sidney Sheldon<br /><br />A Stranger in the Mirror is a 1976 novel written by American writer Sidney Sheldon. The novel is one of the earliest Sheldon's works, but contains the typical Sheldon fast-paced narration and several narrative techniques with the exception of a twist ending. <br /><br />The novel tells the life story of two fictitious Hollywood celebrities - Toby Temple and Jill Castle portray the emotional extremes of success and failure and how people inevitably become victims of time. It was adapted into a television film in 1993 starring Perry King, Lori Loughlin, Christopher Plummer, and Juliet Mills.<br /><br />عنوانها: غریبه ای در آینه؛ غریبه در آینه؛ نویسنده: سیدنی شلدون؛ تاریخ نخستین خوانش: روز هفتم ماه ژانویه سال 1994میلادی<br /><br />عنوان: غریبه ای در آینه؛ نویسنده: سیدنی شلدون؛ مترجم: شاهرخ فرزاد، مشخصات نشر: تهران، شیرین، 1373، در 452ص، چاپ دیگر تهران، درایت، در 452ص؛ 1377؛ شابک 9646370055؛ چاپ دوم درایت 1378؛ موضوع: داستانهای نویسندگان سده 20م<br /><br />عنوان: غریبه ای در آینه؛ نویسنده: سیدنی شلدون؛ مترجم: جعفر صفاری، مشخصات نشر تهران، ارغوان، 1373؛ در 391ص؛ <br /><br />عنوان: غریبه در آینه؛ نویسنده: سیدنی شلدون؛ مترجم: معصومه دریاباری، مشخصات نشر تهران، نشر کستر، 1389؛ در 256ص؛ شابک 9786005883022؛ <br /><br />این رمان، داستان زندگی دو هنرپیشه ی خیالی هالیوود، به نامهای «توبی تمپل» و «جیل کستل» را، بازگو میکند؛ دو هنرپیشه ای که در پیروزی و شکست، چگونگی قربانی شدن انسانها، توسط زمان را، به نمایش میگذارند؛ «توبی تمپل»، یک فوقِ ستاره، و کمدیترین مرد جهان است! هر آنچه را که بخواهد، میتواند صاحب شود؛ اما در پشت ماسک این هنرپیشه ی موفق، چهره ی واقعی یک مردِ تنها نیز، پنهان است؛ «جیل کستل»، زنی جاه طلب، با گذشته ای تاریک، و مرموز است، زنی که با دویست دلار اندوخته اش، در پی روزنه ای، برای ورود به هالیوود، و تبدیل شدن به فوق ستاره ای، همچون «توبی تمپل»، است. زمان برای حکمرانی بر هالیوود، توسط «توبی تمپل»، و «جیل کستل»، فرارسیده است …؛ ا. شربیانی<br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer311615894" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11246584652419868641">This was my first ever Sidney Sheldon book and I loved it. I literally could not put the book down. I slept at 11 pm for three nights and finished it then. The suspense really got me every night and the only thing that kept me from reading was that I knew that I needed to wake up early in the morning. <br/><br/>Never has a book made me feel so much emotions in one time. I felt the passion, the hate, the love, and to be honest, I felt turned on (Blame it on my fourteen year old hormones) at the well-explai</span>
  <span id="freeText11246584652419868641" style="display:none">This was my first ever Sidney Sheldon book and I loved it. I literally could not put the book down. I slept at 11 pm for three nights and finished it then. The suspense really got me every night and the only thing that kept me from reading was that I knew that I needed to wake up early in the morning. <br /><br />Never has a book made me feel so much emotions in one time. I felt the passion, the hate, the love, and to be honest, I felt turned on (Blame it on my fourteen year old hormones) at the well-explained sex scenes.<br /><br />Every word made me want to read the next. Even the prologue made me want to read the whole book that instant. I wanted to find out what would happen to Toby, what would happen to Jill. I saw their transgression from nobodies, one with a huge organ and one I really thought was going to die with her headaches. I loved every minute of it. I loved every minute of reading the book.<br /><br />The last few scenes gave me chills. It was probably due to the fact I was reading at 11 pm. The words were just written so well. I can't even describe how I felt. <br /><br />It really was great and I can't wait to buy another Sidney Sheldon book. The fact that he's a Tony winner made me like him more.<br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_1595979669" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1595979669" />
    <a title="Sumit RK" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/38271102-sumit-rk"><img alt="Sumit RK" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599896274p2/38271102.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1595979669?book_show_action=true">Apr 14, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sumit RK" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sumit RK" href="/user/show/38271102-sumit-rk">Sumit RK</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1595979669" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16847832874804306068">Sidney Sheldon is a master storyteller. His style of storytelling, with fast-paced narration and thrilling scenarios, is unparalleled. A Stranger in the Mirror is also a typical Sheldon novel. <br/><br/> A Stranger in the Mirror is a story that revolves around the life of two characters, namely Toby Temple and Jill Castle. Toby is a small time wannabe comedian who dreams of making it big by entering into the Hollywood. He struggles a lot early on in his life - and transcending all those hardships, goes on</span>
  <span id="freeText16847832874804306068" style="display:none">Sidney Sheldon is a master storyteller. His style of storytelling, with fast-paced narration and thrilling scenarios, is unparalleled. A Stranger in the Mirror is also a typical Sheldon novel. <br /><br /> A Stranger in the Mirror is a story that revolves around the life of two characters, namely Toby Temple and Jill Castle. Toby is a small time wannabe comedian who dreams of making it big by entering into the Hollywood. He struggles a lot early on in his life - and transcending all those hardships, goes on to eventually become a superstar. Jill Castle is a small town girl who grows up watching Hollywood movies and becoming influenced by them, decides to leave for Hollywood. As it is predictable, both their paths cross and a series of events following their meeting forms the rest of the story.<br /><br /> Most of the novel is the story of Toby Temple; from the humble beginnings of Toby Temple, to his long struggle to make a mark in Hollywood, his failures, his struggles, his eventual triumph and his rise to the top of show business and becoming an obnoxious star is a fascinating journey. On a parallel track, we read the story of Jill, her attempts to be a star in Hollywood and the humiliation and disillusionment she faces. The 1950s Hollywood, the ‘behind-the-scenes’ working on a movie set, the making of a star, the efforts and planning that go in making a movie or a TV show are written in great detail and very enjoyable. Sidney Sheldon uses his storytelling skills to keep the reader hooked until the end.<br /><br /> The strangest thing though is that the 2 central characters of the book don’t meet for the first 2/3rds of the book. Even their story together proves anti climatic .Also,the characters and their motivations are the most confusing. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ For eg: Jill goes from being cold hearted &amp; manipulative star to a loving and devoted wife (to a man she hates) and then back to being a cold hearted villain in a matter of days. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> The final parts of novel along with the climax are plain bizarre. From revenge to random characters coming back from nowhere to even some paranormal activities, the climax felt like bit of a mess (when the story could have easily ended on a good note, few chapters back). If you overlook that bit, this is a good story &amp; immensely enjoyable. 3/5</span>
  <a data-text-id="16847832874804306068" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3105204981" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3105204981" />
    <a title="Martina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3939397-martina"><img alt="Martina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1325947875p2/3939397.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3105204981?book_show_action=true">Dec 28, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Martina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Martina" href="/user/show/3939397-martina">Martina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3939397-martina?shelf=thriller">thriller</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3105204981" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9911859056911306842"><i>A stranger in the mirror</i> is the weakest offering from Sheldon's opus that I've read thus far. Just like Sheldon's other books, it's written in an engaging way, so the pages flew by even though I wasn't entranced by the plot. <br/><br/>The novel follows the lives of Toby Temple and Jill Castle, both of which are children of immigrants who want to make it big in Hollywood. Their trials and tribulations prior to meeting each other are chronicled in extensive (and pretty disgusting) detail. When they do meet </span>
  <span id="freeText9911859056911306842" style="display:none"><i>A stranger in the mirror</i> is the weakest offering from Sheldon's opus that I've read thus far. Just like Sheldon's other books, it's written in an engaging way, so the pages flew by even though I wasn't entranced by the plot. <br /><br />The novel follows the lives of Toby Temple and Jill Castle, both of which are children of immigrants who want to make it big in Hollywood. Their trials and tribulations prior to meeting each other are chronicled in extensive (and pretty disgusting) detail. When they do meet each other (at the 2/3 mark of the book), the real plot of the novel begins. After that, the novel unfolds with break-neck speed, which sacrifices character growth. Apart from the pacing problem, there were several moments which required a huge suspension of disbelief...<br /><br />Overall, I'm not a fan of this novel. Stories connected with Hollywood are always such a downer. Perhaps in the seventies this story was fresh and new, but nowadays, knowing all that we know of Hollywood (not to mention the number one problem there), it doesn't bring anything new to the table. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9911859056911306842" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1815732776" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1815732776" />
    <a title="Bren" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/61659069-bren"><img alt="Bren" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590193281p2/61659069.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1815732776?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Bren" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Bren" href="/user/show/61659069-bren">Bren</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780446356572" href="/book/show/580284.A_Stranger_in_the_Mirror">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/61659069-bren?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/61659069-bren?shelf=california">california</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/61659069-bren?shelf=multiple-reads-reread-at-least-once">multiple-reads-reread-at-least-once</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/61659069-bren?shelf=chick-lit">chick-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/61659069-bren?shelf=fantastic-book-covers">fantastic-book-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/61659069-bren?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/61659069-bren?shelf=dark-and-heavy">dark-and-heavy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/61659069-bren?shelf=read-and-reviewed">read-and-reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1815732776" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8287936876760416692">“They had lied. Time was not a friend that healed all wounds ;it was the enemy that ravaged and murdered youth.” <br/>― Sidney Sheldon, A Stranger in the Mirror<br/><br/><br/><br/>Of all Sheldon's books, this is among my favorites. It is pretty different from most of his other works.<br/><br/>So this book is about two people. One of them is Toby Temple. Toby is one of the biggest comedians in the world. He was born to make people laugh. His fans love him. The world loves him.<br/><br/>But Toby is also one of the world's loneliest people. H</span>
  <span id="freeText8287936876760416692" style="display:none">“They had lied. Time was not a friend that healed all wounds ;it was the enemy that ravaged and murdered youth.” <br />― Sidney Sheldon, A Stranger in the Mirror<br /><br /><br /><br />Of all Sheldon's books, this is among my favorites. It is pretty different from most of his other works.<br /><br />So this book is about two people. One of them is Toby Temple. Toby is one of the biggest comedians in the world. He was born to make people laugh. His fans love him. The world loves him.<br /><br />But Toby is also one of the world's loneliest people. He cannot relate to other human beings. He has dozens of friends but nobody he confides in. He is a bit like a lost puppy. He has everything most people strive for and still he is alone.<br /><br />Then there is Jill Castle. Formerly named Josie (she changed it) Jill comes to Hollywood as an aspiring actress. She is bubbly, enthusiastic and fearless about making it in her chosen field. Filled with love and desperately seeking distance from a relationship gone wrong, she is hoping to be Hollywood's next big thing.<br /><br />Things however are not working out for Jill. Nobody wants to hire her and when she suffers a horrifying incident it changes her. She becomes hard and cold and will do anything to make it on the big screen.<br /><br />That's the backdrop. The book is really about the meeting of these two characters. They are both two lonely, very jaded, sad individuals. When their paths collide, what happens next will change both their lives.<br /><br />This story is a human tragedy. I was very drawn to Toby. When he's bad he's very bad, but when he's good, he is amazing. His character is unique and I loved reading about him.<br /><br />Jill is fascinating in her own way. It is odd how the reader will feel sympathy for her and then possibly come to dislike or even hate her. Yet her changes are presented in a very realistic and human way.<br /><br />There are no major Sheldon twists in this novel. It is, in some ways, a character story, although a twisted one. It is unlike virtually anything I have read by him and I happily give it five stars.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8287936876760416692" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5341288342880709338">Mr. Sheldon does it again! Another breathtaking story about love, betrayal, vengeance and murder. This is bit different than his other books but I really enjoyed it.<br/><br/>Toby grew up with an idea that he was born to be famous. On the other hand, Jill grew up dreaming about being rich and beautiful.   <span id="freeText5341288342880709338" style="display:none">Mr. Sheldon does it again! Another breathtaking story about love, betrayal, vengeance and murder. This is bit different than his other books but I really enjoyed it.<br /><br />Toby grew up with an idea that he was born to be famous. On the other hand, Jill grew up dreaming about being rich and beautiful. Soon, both realize that the only place that gives them what they want is Hollywood.<br /><br />Both of them have to struggle to reach to the top. The part that describes their struggle is really heart touching. They have to lie, face humiliation, get rejected and sell their bodies until they get chance. Soon Toby becomes the superstar and the king of Hollywood but Jill is still struggling until one day they cross each other's path. Despite their age difference, they fall in love. Toby wants to marry Jill because she was the only girl who ever rejected him but Jill wants him because getting Toby's power is the only way to punish all the people who have used and rejected her.<br /><br />They rise and rise as a Golden Couple of Hollywood until the love turns into betrayal and betrayal influences vengeance. The hounding carries on until they come together again, and until their love story is written forever by the stars that are only visible to soft night wind and the timeless sea.<br /><br />Sidney Sheldon gets 5 out of 5 again from me.<br /><br />Published on <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pchhantyal.blogspot.in/2014/10/a-stranger-in-mirror-by-sidney-sheldon.html">http://pchhantyal.blogspot.in/2014/10...</a></span>

<div id="review_426888753" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Graceann" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Graceann" href="/user/show/643332-graceann">Graceann</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780446356572" href="/book/show/580284.A_Stranger_in_the_Mirror">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/643332-graceann?shelf=trashy-fiction">trashy-fiction</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer426888753" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3783876690164603035">Ah, Sidney Sheldon, what can you say about him? His novels are trashy, full of unrealistic, rather silly plots, sex and situations ... and they are so un-putdownable that they might as well be made of crazy glue. <br/><br/>In this one, two young aspiring performers have simultaneous stories. Toby Temple is a young comic with a boyish, innocent face but a mean streak a mile deep. Jill Castle has had to fight and claw to get any sort of career. <br/><br/>This one gets three stars rather than just one because the stor</span>
  <span id="freeText3783876690164603035" style="display:none">Ah, Sidney Sheldon, what can you say about him? His novels are trashy, full of unrealistic, rather silly plots, sex and situations ... and they are so un-putdownable that they might as well be made of crazy glue. <br /><br />In this one, two young aspiring performers have simultaneous stories. Toby Temple is a young comic with a boyish, innocent face but a mean streak a mile deep. Jill Castle has had to fight and claw to get any sort of career. <br /><br />This one gets three stars rather than just one because the story genuinely surprised me and it was immensely readable and enjoyable to me. There was stuff, especially in the last third, that I simply did not see coming and I loved how Sheldon pulled it all together. It gets three stars instead of five because of the clunky pacing in the first half and the ridiculously schmaltzy romantic language. <br /><br />It's like cotton candy - I'll have forgotten the characters' names by next week (actually, I had to look up Jill's last name just to write this review). But I love cotton candy. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3783876690164603035" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2596994103" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2596994103" />
    <a title="Shivam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/89443205-shivam"><img alt="Shivam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1547025226p2/89443205.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2596994103?book_show_action=true">Nov 26, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shivam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shivam" href="/user/show/89443205-shivam">Shivam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2596994103" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5590274382985218639">'A Stranger in the Mirror' is sure to stir-up a maelstrom of emotions in your living, heavenly bodies! A classic rags to riches story that pays great tribute to not only the Makers of their destiny but also to the Survivors who cling onto their hopes and desires to the very climax of their lives!<br/><br/>Toby Temple, a nobody, chases his dreams with all that he has, as his talent and sacrifices (and years of hard work) pave way to the incredible allure of Hollywood, thus making him the undisputed King.<br/><br/>Ji</span>
  <span id="freeText5590274382985218639" style="display:none">'A Stranger in the Mirror' is sure to stir-up a maelstrom of emotions in your living, heavenly bodies! A classic rags to riches story that pays great tribute to not only the Makers of their destiny but also to the Survivors who cling onto their hopes and desires to the very climax of their lives!<br /><br />Toby Temple, a nobody, chases his dreams with all that he has, as his talent and sacrifices (and years of hard work) pave way to the incredible allure of Hollywood, thus making him the undisputed King.<br /><br />Jill Castle has had her life wrapped up in religion and social stigmas from which she is trying to break free to search for love, stardom and glory!<br /><br />Sidney Sheldon comprehensively and masterfully crafts a storyline bringing the two protagonists together and focuses on the workings of showbiz as the two leads 'get together', and ultimately fall apart (and how!). The quest for fame and power and how it makes you despise yourself and loathe those around you has found the author's attention, and has been suffused throughout the book. The reader 'grows' with the characters, visualising them change and discover as they reach the epitome of Business, and lead to their respective destruction.<br /><br />The author takes special care to paint a mirror image of one's own self, as we drive through life taking it head on! We all have a stranger living within ourselves. The stranger who is frail as a living entity, who dives through the struggles and the victories in life, and who reaches the unavoidable grand finale: Death. And the more he tries to run away from it, the more he becomes 'it'.<br /><br />The book is "psychologically moving", and if adapted for the screen today, would still make a better overall product than a LA LA LAND.<br /><br />Rating - 3.75/5</span>
  <a data-text-id="5590274382985218639" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText4253472767933921528" style="display:none">Book name:- A Stranger In The Mirror .<br />Author:- Sidney Sheldon .<br />This book actually gave me goosebumps 😖 . It has mainly highlighted the dark side of the Hollywood and people associated with the industry . It portraits the real lives of the renowned stars and what were the challenges they had to face in their journey to fame . The "so-called" overnight stars also have years of struggles which gets overshadowed by their success. We all talk about how shinning and glamorous celebrities are but in reality how dark is their real world is . .<br />*<br />.Main Characters :- *<br />Toby Temple:- A superstar, a comedian and an actor. He gets any women he wants. But underneath the callous super stud image is a lonely man , desperate for attention, greedy for love . He absconded from his home at an young age to achieve the dream that his mother predicted for him . And after years of struggle and hard work he becomes the King of Hollywood. . *<br />Jill Castle:- Beautiful, sensuous starlet. She has a dark and mysterious past and an ambition even greater then Toby's. Her struggles to get at least an apperance in a movie was much more torturous . She had to face casting couch not once or twice but several times . Her tough situations made her even more and ambitious and rebellious. . *<br />Later Jill Castle became Jill Temple (married to Toby Temple) . Together they could have lived happily ever after . But when revenge and jealousy occupies your mind you forget everything that matters. *<br />...................<br />What happens after Jill marries Toby ? How does she become Mrs . Temple and became the queen of Hollywood? What is her mysterious past ? ............<br />To know the answer to this mysterious, dark , sorrowful novel by Sidney Sheldon you have to go through this book 😌<br />.............................</span>

<div id="review_2947879110" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2947879110" />
    <a title="Susan Liston" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/630381-susan-liston"><img alt="Susan Liston" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1414603470p2/630381.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2947879110?book_show_action=true">Aug 22, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Susan Liston" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Susan Liston" href="/user/show/630381-susan-liston">Susan Liston</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780688030025" href="/book/show/1834389.A_Stranger_in_the_Mirror">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/630381-susan-liston?shelf=read-2019">read-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/630381-susan-liston?shelf=vintage-trashy">vintage-trashy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2947879110" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14324962356760799557">I read a lot of non-fiction, and occasionally I need an escapist break. I've been trying and trying current "thrillers" which I keep finding to be derivative, badly written tripe. Why not try some older stuff that is unabashedly trashy? Books by these authors, like Sheldon and Harold Robbins, Irving Wallace, were all over the place when I was young but I was not allowed to read them, now I'm a grownup (technically) I can. And yes, this book was utterly, completely ridiculous but I did enjoy it. </span>
  <span id="freeText14324962356760799557" style="display:none">I read a lot of non-fiction, and occasionally I need an escapist break. I've been trying and trying current "thrillers" which I keep finding to be derivative, badly written tripe. Why not try some older stuff that is unabashedly trashy? Books by these authors, like Sheldon and Harold Robbins, Irving Wallace, were all over the place when I was young but I was not allowed to read them, now I'm a grownup (technically) I can. And yes, this book was utterly, completely ridiculous but I did enjoy it. In fact, near the end when we find out a shocking thing <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[David's sister wasn't raped, he caught her having consensual sex with the Mexican gardener, stabs the poor man to death and has his sister committed to an insane asylum FOR LIFE. Now is that more sexist than racist, or more racist than sexist? Is it a draw? Had I not been overcome with laughter I might have decided <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I actually shrieked and got a good five minute laugh out of it. Just great. Since these books were supposed to be "racy" there is a lot of sexual content meant to shock, I think, but it's all seems rather juvenile/crude now. Overall, very silly, but fun.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14324962356760799557" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3303573758" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3303573758" />
    <a title="Sharon" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25065000-sharon"><img alt="Sharon" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3303573758?book_show_action=true">Apr 26, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon" href="/user/show/25065000-sharon">Sharon</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3303573758" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10949255363929692266">Compared to the other Sheldons I have read, this one was quite disappointing. It brought in the possibility of supernatural behavior and had a story line that just didn't ring true to me in any sense. I didn't believe that each of the people reached the unrealistic goals they had set for themselves, that they had such mean streaks or that they would react the way they did. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('TSoC/YaQPpy9WflZx8LJGMqOVFMRqq0pK8zMQ4EuxIEVh5hLV/w/IC802sdSINvoRDqLGBP7h7wEnZIwasla3w==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+XLndF6p4nyZLPL4Y82PS8CH/NQb7PjJ306qjKdcaMGh333Cj8XjwAtB0Wb2L527TjMjnxm90lzwH/T/TLv2nw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer16098954514485343936">Sidney Sheldon (1917-2007) was an American writer who won awards in three careers—a Broadway playwright, a Hollywood TV and movie screenwriter, and a best-selling novelist.<br/><br/>His TV works spanned a twenty-year period during which he created <i>I Dream of Jeannie</i> (1965-70), <i>Hart to Hart</i> (1979-84), and <i>The Patty Duke Show</i> (1963-66), but it was not until after he turned 50 and began writing best-selling no</span>
  <span id="freeText16098954514485343936" style="display:none">Sidney Sheldon (1917-2007) was an American writer who won awards in three careers—a Broadway playwright, a Hollywood TV and movie screenwriter, and a best-selling novelist.<br /><br />His TV works spanned a twenty-year period during which he created <i>I Dream of Jeannie</i> (1965-70), <i>Hart to Hart</i> (1979-84), and <i>The Patty Duke Show</i> (1963-66), but it was not until after he turned 50 and began writing best-selling novels such as <i>Master of the Game</i> (1982), <i>The Other Side of Midnight</i> (1973) and <i>Rage of Angels</i> (1980) that he became most famous.</span>
